  <script>
   let firstHiddenTime = document.visibilityState === 'hidden' ? 0 : Infinity;
        document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', (event) => {
          firstHiddenTime = Math.min(firstHiddenTime, event.timeStamp);
        }, {once: true});

        try {
          let lcp;

          function updateLCP(entry) {
            if (entry.startTime < firstHiddenTime) {
              lcp = entry.startTime;
              console.log('- lcp:', entry.startTime, entry.element)
            }
          }

          const po = new PerformanceObserver((entryList, po) => {
            entryList.getEntries().forEach((entry) => updateLCP(entry, po));
          });

          po.observe({
            type: 'largest-contentful-paint',
            buffered: true,
          });

          addEventListener('visibilitychange', function fn(event) {
            if (document.visibilityState === 'hidden') {
              removeEventListener('visibilitychange', fn, true);

              po.takeRecords().forEach((entry) => updateLCP(entry, po));
              po.disconnect();
            }
          }, true);
        } catch (e) {}
  </script>

  <script>
   function sendVitalsToDataLayer (label) {
          return function (data) {
            const multiplier = label === 'LCP' ? 1: 1000
            const valueInMS = Math.round(data.value * multiplier)
            window.dataLayer.push({
              event: 'web vitals ' + label,
              vitals: valueInMS
            })
          }
        }

        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
          webVitals.getCLS(sendVitalsToDataLayer('CLS'));
          webVitals.getFID(sendVitalsToDataLayer('FID'));
          webVitals.getLCP(sendVitalsToDataLayer('LCP'));
          webVitals.getFCP(sendVitalsToDataLayer('FCP'));
          webVitals.getTTFB(sendVitalsToDataLayer('TTFB'));
        });
  </script>

          loadReve()
      }, 2500)
 </script>

      let isAppLazyLoaded = false;
      // value will get replaced in fundation
      const LAZY_LOAD_TIMER = 5000;
      const lazyLoadEvents = ['mousedown', 'scroll', 'touchstart'];

      function lazyLoadApp () {
        if (isAppLazyLoaded) {
          return;
        }

        isAppLazyLoaded = true;

        // do not remove, keyword is getting str.replaced in fundation
        function insertAfter(el, referenceNode) {referenceNode.parentNode.insertBefore(el, referenceNode.nextSibling);}
      var lastScript = document.querySelector('script[data-id="lg-pagespeed"]');

      [[]].forEach(function(src){
        var s = document.createElement("script"); s.setAttribute("async", true); s.src = src; insertAfter(s, lastScript);
        lastScript = s;
      });

      if (window.location.search.indexOf('vue=false') === -1 &&
        1
      ) {
        ['"/dist/manifest_1e6aa82d07cf98812279.js','"/dist/vendors~app_1e6aa82d07cf98812279.js','"/dist/app_1e6aa82d07cf98812279.js'].forEach(function(src){
          src=src.replace('"', '')
          var s = document.createElement("script"); s.setAttribute("crossorigin", "anonymous"); s.setAttribute("async", true); s.src = src; insertAfter(s, lastScript);
          lastScript = s;
        });
      }

        lazyLoadEvents.forEach(event => {
          // 'mousedown', 'scroll', 'touchstart'
          window.removeEventListener(event, lazyLoadApp)
        })
      }

      lazyLoadEvents.forEach(event => {
        // 'mousedown', 'scroll', 'touchstart'
        window.addEventListener(event, lazyLoadApp)
      })
      setTimeout(lazyLoadApp, LAZY_LOAD_TIMER);
 </script>
